## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed corpus-process bullets stand beside what the sheet implies for transition failures, a resume that surfaces a snapshot-reality mismatch halts continuation and repairs the journal first, a handoff whose successor reports gaps triggers a corrected handoff note from the leaver while context survives, a failed quality audit executes its own remedy, the corrected checkpoint, and repeated gaps from one template's outputs indict the calibration choice, not the template system
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because every response routes failure back into the journal rather than around it, the family's single-source-of-truth design means transition failures are journal failures wearing transition clothes, and the repairs all write journal entries
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the erosion path is compensating outside the system, successors patching gaps by asking the leaver directly, effective once and corrosive always, the side channel replacing the record until the next successor has neither

## Section 022: Observability Checklist
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the contract gives metrics a standing field and the playbook makes them a handoff item, but fields go hollow without inspection, and the audit question is the family's only mechanism that actively notices a hollow metrics field
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: without the question, metrics decay is the family's most silent rot, the field persists, entries fill it with nothing, and the first regression investigation finds a year of blanks where baselines should be

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed task-splitting bounds stand beside the sheet's own scale limits, each template covers one transition of one workstream, scaling by invocation count rather than by template growth, the grid covers two directions and two audiences and nothing else, no crisis handoffs, no multi-successor broadcasts, no cross-workstream transfers, and the sheet's authority ends at wording, when transitions happen and what journals contain belong to its siblings
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the templates stay small because each addresses one moment, and moments do not grow with project size, a ten-person project has more transitions, not bigger ones, so the sheet scales linearly by design
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the characteristic scale failure is the broadcast handoff, one note addressed to several successors with different needs, the packet's fields calibrated for one audience serving none, the grid's audience axis silently violated
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: scale limits of the sheet, this evolution's own task splitting keeps the seed paragraphs
- **revision_decision:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to state the three boundaries, per-transition templates, invocation-count scaling, and wording-only authority
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the uncovered genres are compositions, not gaps, a crisis handoff is the developer template at maximum honesty under time pressure, a multi-successor transfer is the packet template invoked once per successor with per-audience calibration, the grid's four cells compose to cover the long tail, which is why five templates have sufficed without revision

## Section 025: Future Refresh Search Queries
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed theme-name queries would surface generic prompt-engineering chatter while this node's staleness has exact homes, the two checksums and their equality, the sweep inventory that could add a revised sheet or a new family generation, the template inventory and field lists that mechanical checks cover, and the family's reference core whose stability this theme's findings now partly stand on
- **supporting_reason:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because an executable sheet decays structurally, by copies, carriers, and derivatives, not factually, its content names no external subject to drift, so every probe is an archive operation
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: undirected refreshing would miss a sixth template arriving in a future sweep, the one change that would break the closed-grid claim while leaving every current fact intact

- **revision_decision:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to replace name queries with targeted probes, dual checksum runs, template and field counts, a step-one-line grep, and sweep scans keyed on the sheet's title text and the family fingerprint
